});\n  });\n}\n\n// Handle context menu clicks\nchrome.contextMenus.onClicked.addListener(async (info, tab) => {\n  switch (info.menuItemId) {\n    case \'create-proof-page\':\n      await true, currentWindow: true });\n  \n  switch (command) {\n    case \'create-proof\':\n      await createProofOfPage(tab);\n      break;\n    case \'verify-proof\':\n      await verifyProofFromClipboard(tab);\n      break;\n  }\n});\n\n// Handle messages from popup and content scripts\nchrome.runtime.onMessage.addListener((request, sender, sendResponse) => {\n  (async () => {\n    try {\n      switch (request.action) {\n        case \'createProof\':\n          const proof = await createProof(request.data);\n          sendResponse({ success: true, proof });\n          break;\n        \n        case \'verifyProof\':\n          const verification = await verifyProof(request.proofId);\n          sendResponse({ success: true, verification });\n          break;\n        \n        case \'getAuthToken\':\n          sendResponse({ success: true, token: authToken });\n          break;\n        \n        case \'setAuthToken\':\n          authToken = request.token;\n   // Show success notification\n    showNotification(\'Proof Created\', `Proof of "${pageData.title}" created successfully!`);\n    \n    // Copy proof link to clipboard\n    await proof.\');\n  }\n}\n\n// Create proof of image\nasync function createProofOfImage(imageUrl, tab) {\n  try {\n    // Download image as blob\n    const response = await fetch(imageUrl);\n    const blob   metadata: {\n        source: imageUrl,\n        page: tab.url,\n        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n      }\n    });\n    \n    showNotification(\'Proof Created\', \'Proof of image image.\');\n  }\n}\n\n// Create proof of link\nasync function createProofOfLink(linkUrl, tab) {\n  try {\n    const proof = await createProof({\n      type: \'link\',\n      content: linkUrl,\n      metadata: {\n        source: tab.url,\n        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n      }\n    });\n    \n    showNotification(\'Proof Created\', \'Proof of link created!\');\n    await copyToClipboard(proof.proof_link);\n    \n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\'Error creating proof:\', error);\n    showNotification(\'Error\', \'Failed to create proof.\');\n  }\n}\n\n// Verify proof from clipboard\nasync function verifyProofFromClipboard(tab) {\n  try {\n    // Read from clipboard\n    const text = await navigator.clipboard.readText();\n    \n    // Extract proof ID from URL or text\n    const proofId = extractProofId(text);\n    \n    if (!proofId) {\n      showNotification(\'Error\', \'No valid proof link found in clipboard.\');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Verify proof\n    const verification = await verifyProof(proofId);\n    \n    if (verification.valid) {\n      showNotification(\'Proof Valid ‚úì\', `Verified on ${new Date(verification.timestamp).toLocaleString()}`);\n    } else {\n      showNotification(\'Proof Invalid ‚úó\', \'This proof could not be verified.\');\n    }\n    \n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\'Error verifying proof:\', error);\n    showNotification(\'Error\', \'Failed to verify proof.\');\n  }\n}\n\n// API Functions\nasync function createProof(data) {\n  const response = await fetch(`${apiUrl}/proofs`, {\n    method: \'POST\',\n    headers: {\n      \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\',\n      \'Authorization\': authToken ? `Bearer ${authToken}` : \'\'\n    },\n    body: JSON.stringify(data)\n  });\n  \n  if (!response.ok) {\n    throw new Error(\'Failed to create proof\');\n  }\n  \n  return await response.json();\n}\n\nasync function verifyProof(proofId) {\n  const response = await fetch(`${apiUrl}/proofs/${proofId}/verify`, {\n    method: \'GET\',\n    headers: {\n      \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\'\n    }\n  });\n  \n  if (!response.ok) {\n    throw new Error(\'Failed to verify proof\');\n  }\n  \n  return await response.json();\n}\n\n// Helper Functions\nfunction extractProofId(text) {\n  // Try to extract from URL\n  const urlMatch = text.match(/prooflink\\.ai\\/verify\\/([a-zA-Z0-9-]+)/);\n  if (urlMatch) return urlMatch[1];\n  \n  // Try to extract UUID\n  const uuidMatch = text.match(/[a-f0-9]{8}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{12}/i);\n  if (uuidMatch) return uuidMatch[0];\n  \n  return null;\n}\n\nasync function copyToClipboard(text) {\n  await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);\n}\n\nfunction blobToBase64(blob) {\n  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {\n    const reader = new FileReader();\n    reader.onloadend = () => resolve(reader.result);\n    reader.onerror = reject;\n    reader.readAsDataURL(blob);\n  });\n}\n\nfunction showNotification(title, message) {\n  chrome.notifications.create({\n    type: \'basic\',\n    iconUrl: \'../icons/icon128.png\',\n    title,\n    message\n  });\n}\n\n// Keep service worker alive\nchrome.runtime.onStartup.addListener(() => {\n  console.log(\'ProofLink.AI extension started\');\n});\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

token } = await chrome.runtime.sendMessage({ action: \'getAuthToken\' });\n    \n    if (token) {\n      showMainSection();\n      await loadStats();\n      await loadRecentProofs();\n    } else {\n      showAuthSection();\n    }\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\'Error initializing popup:\', error);\n    showAuthSection();\n  }\n}\n\n// Show auth section\nfunction showAuthSection() {\n  authSection.style.display = \'block\';\n  mainSection.style.display = \'none\';\n}\n\n// Show main section\nfunction showMainSection() {\n  authSection.style.display = \'none\';\n  mainSection.style.display = \'block\';\n}\n\n// Load user stats\nasync function loadStats() {\n  try {\n    const { token } = await chrome.runtime.sendMessage({ action: \'getAuthToken\' });\n    \n    const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/users/me/stats`, {\n      headers: {\n        \'Authorization\': `Bearer ${token}`\n      }\n    });\n    \n    if (response.ok) {\n      const stats = await response.json();\n      totalProofsEl.textContent = stats.total_proofs || 0;\n      thisMonthEl.textContent = stats.this_month || 0;\n    }\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\'Error loading stats:\', error);\n  }\n}\n\n// Load recent proofs\nasync function loadRecentProofs() {\n  try {\n    const { token } = await chrome.runtime.sendMessage({ action: \'getAuthToken\' });\n    \n    const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/proofs?limit=5`, {\n      headers: {\n        \'Authorization\': `Bearer ${token}`\n      }\n    });\n    \n    if (response.ok) {\n      const proofs = await response.json();\n      displayRecentProofs(proofs);\n    }\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\'Error loading recent proofs:\', error);\n  }\n}\n\n// Display recent proofs\nfunction displayRecentProofs(proofs) {\n  if (!proofs || proofs.length === 0) {\n    recentProofsEl.innerHTML = `\n      <div class="empty-state">\n        <p>No proofs yet</p>\n        <p class="empty-hint">Create your first proof above</p>\n      </div>\n    `;\n    return;\n  }\n  \n  recentProofsEl.innerHTML = proofs.map(proof => `\n    <div class="recent-item" data-proof-id="${proof.id}">\n      <div class="recent-item-title">${proof.title || \'Untitled Proof\'}</div>\n      <div class="recent-item-meta">\n        <span class="recent-item-type">${proof.type}</span>\n        <span>${formatDate(proof.created_at)}</span>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  `).join(\'\');\n  \n  // Add click handlers\n  document.querySelectorAll(\'.recent-item\').forEach(item => {\n    item.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n      const proofId = item.dataset.proofId;\n      openProofLink(proofId);\n    });\n  });\n}\n\n// Format date\nfunction formatDate(dateString) {\n  const date = new Date(dateString);\n  const now = new Date();\n  const diff = now - date;\n  \n  const minutes = Math.floor(diff / 60000);\n  const hours = Math.floor(diff / 3600000);\n  const days = Math.floor(diff / 86400000);\n  \n  if (minutes < 1) return \'Just now\';\n  if (minutes < 60) return `${minutes}m ago`;\n  if (hours < 24) return `${hours}h ago`;\n  if (days < 7) return `${days}d ago`;\n  \n  return date.toLocaleDateString();\n}\n\n// Open proof link\nfunction openProofLink(proofId) {\n  chrome.tabs.create({\n    url: `https://prooflink.ai/verify/${proofId}`\n  });\n}\n\n// Event Listeners\nloginBtn.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n  chrome.tabs.create({\n    url: \'https://prooflink.ai/auth/login\'\n  });\n});\n\nregisterBtn.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n  chrome.tabs.create({\n    url: \'https://prooflink.ai/auth/register\'\n  });\n});\n\nproofPageBtn.addEventListener(\'click\', async () => {\n  try {\n    const [tab] = await chrome.tabs.query({ active: true, currentWindow: true });\n    \n    // Send message to background script\n    chrome.runtime.sendMessage({\n      action: \'createProof\',\n      data: {\n        type: \'webpage\',\n        url: tab.url,\n        title: tab.title\n      }\n    }, (response) => {\n      if (response.success) {\n        showSuccess(\'Proof created successfully!\');\n        loadStats();\n        loadRecentProofs();\n      } else {\n        showError(\'Failed to create proof\');\n      }\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\'Error creating proof:\', error);\n    showError(\'Failed to create proof\');\n  }\n});\n\nproofSelectionBtn.addEventListener(\'click\', async () => {\n  try {\n    const [tab] = await chrome.tabs.query({ active: true, currentWindow: true });\n    \n    // Get selected text from content script\n    const response = await chrome.tabs.sendMessage(tab.id, {\n      action: \'captureSelection\'\n    });\n    \n    if (response.selection) {\n      chrome.runtime.sendMessage({\n        action: \'createProof\',\n        data: {\n          type: \'text\',\n          content: response.selection\n        }\n      }, (response) => {\n        if (response.success) {\n          showSuccess(\'Proof created successfully!\');\n          loadStats();\n          loadRecentProofs();\n        } else {\n          showError(\'Failed to create proof\');\n        }\n      });\n    } else {\n      showError(\'No text selected\');\n    }\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\'Error creating proof:\', error);\n    showError(\'Please select some text first\');\n  }\n});\n\nverifyBtn.addEventListener(\'click\', async () => {\n  try {\n    const text = await navigator.clipboard.readText();\n    \n    chrome.runtime.sendMessage({\n      action: \'verifyProof\',\n      proofId: extractProofId(text)\n    }, (response) => {\n      if (response.success && response.verification.valid) {\n        showSuccess(\'Proof is valid!\');\n      } else {\n        showError(\'Proof is invalid or not found\');\n      }\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\'Error verifying proof:\', error);\n    showError(\'Failed to verify proof\');\n  }\n});\n\nsettingsBtn.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n  chrome.runtime.openOptionsPage();\n});\n\ndashboardBtn.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n  chrome.tabs.create({\n    url: \'https://prooflink.ai/dashboard\'\n  });\n});\n\n// Helper functions\nfunction extractProofId(text) {\n  const urlMatch = text.match(/prooflink\\.ai\\/verify\\/([a-zA-Z0-9-]+)/);\n  if (urlMatch) return urlMatch[1];\n  \n  const uuidMatch = text.match(/[a-f0-9]{8}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{4}-[a-f0-9]{12}/i);\n  if (uuidMatch) return uuidMatch[0];\n  \n  return null;\n}\n\nfunction showSuccess(message) {\n  const notification = document.createElement(\'div\');\n  notification.className = \'notification success\';\n  notification.textContent = message;\n  document.body.appendChild(notification);\n  \n  setTimeout(() => {\n    notification.remove();\n  }, 3000);\n}\n\nfunction showError(message) {\n  const notification = document.createElement(\'div\');\n  notification.className = \'notification error\';\n  notification.textContent = message;\n  document.body.appendChild(notification);\n  \n  setTimeout(() => {\n    notification.remove();\n  }, 3000);\n}\n\n// Initialize on load\ninit();\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

class="help-text">Sign in to sync your proofs across devices</p>\n      `;\n      logoutBtn.style.display = \'none\';\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    const response = await accountInfo.innerHTML = `\n        <p><strong>Email:</strong> ${user.email}</p>\n        <p><strong>Plan:</strong> ${user.subscription_tier || \'Free\'}</p>\n        <p><strong>Member since:</strong> <p>Not signed in</p>\n      <p class="help-text">Sign in to sync your proofs across devices</p>\n    `;\n    logoutBtn.style.display = \'none\';\n  }\n}\n\n// Save settings\nasync function saveSettings() {\n  try {\n    const settings = {\n      apiUrl: apiUrlInput.value.trim() || defaultSettings.apiUrl,\n      apiKey: apiKeyInput.value.trim(),\n      notificationsEnabled: notificationsEnabled.checked,\n      autoCopy: autoCopy.checked,\n      analytics: analytics.checked\n    };\n    \n    await chrome.storage.sync.set(settings);\n    \n    // Update background statusMessage.className = `status-message ${type}`;\n  \n  setTimeout(() => {\n    statusMessage.className = \'status-message\';\n  }, 3000);\n}\n\n// Event saveSettings);\nautoCopy.addEventListener(\'change\', saveSettings);\nanalytics.addEventListener(\'change\', saveSettings);\n\n// Initialize on alert: HighErrorRate\n        expr: rate(http_requests_total{status=~"5.."}[5m]) > 0.05\n        for: 5m\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n        annotations:\n          summary: "High error rate detected"\n          description: "Error rate is {{ $value }} errors/sec for {{ $labels.instance }}"\n\n      # API Response Time\n      - alert: HighResponseTime\n        expr: histogram_quantile(0.95, rate(http_request_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) > 1\n        for: 5m\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n        annotations:\n          summary: "High API response time"\n          description: "95th percentile response time is {{ $value }}s for {{ $labels.instance }}"\n\n      # Database Connection Pool\n      - alert: ServiceDown\n        expr: up == 0\n        for: 2m\n        labels:\n          severity: critical\n        annotations:\n          summary: "Service is down"\n          description: "{{ $labels.job }} on {{ $labels.instance }} is down"\n\n      # High CPU Usage\n      - alert: HighCPUUsage\n        expr: 100 - (avg by(instance) (rate(node_cpu_seconds_total{mode="idle"}[5m])) * 100) > 80\n        for: 5m\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n        annotations:\n          summary: "High CPU usage"\n          description: "CPU usage is {{ $value }}% on {{ $labels.instance }}"\n\n      # High Memory Usage\n      - alert: HighMemoryUsage\n        expr: (1 - (node_memory_MemAvailable_bytes / node_memory_MemTotal_bytes)) > 0.9\n        for: 5m\n        labels:\n          severity: warning\n        annotations:\n          summary: "High memory usage"\n          description: "Memory usage is {{ $value | humanizePercentage }} on {{ $labels.instance }}"\n\n      # SSL Certificate Expiry\n      - {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="prooflink/deployment/restore.sh">\n#!/bin/bash\n\n# ProofLink.AI Restore Script\n# This script restores backups of the database and uploaded files\n\nset -e\n\n# Check arguments\nif [ $# -lt 1 ]; then\n    echo "Usage: $0 <timestamp>"\n    echo "Example: $0 20240115_120000"\n    echo ""\n    echo "Available backups:"\n    ls -lh /backups/db_backup_*.sql.gz 2>/dev/null | awk \'{print $9}\' | sed \'s/.*db_backup_//\' | sed \'s/.sql.gz//\'\n    exit 1\nfi\n\nTIMESTAMP=$1\nBACKUP_DIR="/backups"\n\n# Verify backups exist\nif [ ! -f "${BACKUP_DIR}/db_backup_${TIMESTAMP}.sql.gz" ]; then\n    echo "Error: Database backup not found: db_backup_${TIMESTAMP}.sql.gz"\n    exit 1\nfi\n\nif [ ! -f "${BACKUP_DIR}/uploads_backup_${TIMESTAMP}.tar.gz" ]; then\n    echo "Error: Uploads backup not found: uploads_backup_${TIMESTAMP}.tar.gz"\n    exit 1\nfi\n\n# Confirm restore\necho "WARNING: This will overwrite current data!"\necho "Restoring from backup: ${TIMESTAMP}"\nread -p "Are you sure? (yes/no): " confirm\n\nif [ "$confirm" != "yes" ]; then\n    echo "Restore cancelled."\n    exit 0\nfi\n\n# Stop services\necho "Stopping services..."\ndocker-compose stop backend frontend\n\n# Restore database\necho "Restoring database..."\ngunzip -c "${BACKUP_DIR}/db_backup_${TIMESTAMP}.sql.gz" | docker exec -i prooflink-postgres psql -U prooflink prooflink\necho "Database restored successfully!"\n\n# Restore uploads\necho "Restoring uploads..."\ndocker run --rm -v prooflink_upload_data:/data -v ${BACKUP_DIR}:/backup alpine sh -c "rm -rf /data/* && tar xzf /backup/uploads_backup_${TIMESTAMP}.tar.gz -C /data"\necho "Uploads restored successfully!"\n\n# Restore Redis (optional)\nif [ -f "${BACKUP_DIR}/redis_backup_${TIMESTAMP}.rdb" ]; then\n    echo "Restoring Redis..."\n    docker cp "${BACKUP_DIR}/redis_backup_${TIMESTAMP}.rdb" prooflink-redis:/data/dump.rdb\n    docker restart prooflink-redis\n    echo "Redis restored successfully!"\nfi\n\n# Start services\necho "Starting services..."\ndocker-compose start backend frontend\n\necho "Restore completed successfully!"\necho "Please verify the application is working correctly."\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="prooflink/deployment/DEPLOYMENT_RUNBOOK.md">\n# ProofLink.AI Deployment Runbook\n\n## Table of Contents\n1. [Prerequisites](#prerequisites)\n2. [Initial Setup](#initial-setup)\n3. [Docker Deployment](#docker-deployment)\n4. [Kubernetes Deployment](#kubernetes-deployment)\n5. [Monitoring Setup](#monitoring-setup)\n6. [Backup & Recovery](#backup--recovery)\n7. [Troubleshooting](#troubleshooting)\n8. [Maintenance](#maintenance)\n\n---\n\n## Prerequisites\n\n### Required Software\n- Docker 20.10+\n- Docker Compose 2.0+\n- kubectl 1.24+ (for Kubernetes)\n- Git\n\n### Required Accounts\n- Domain registrar (for DNS)\n- SSL certificate provider (or Let\'s Encrypt)\n- Stripe account (for payments)\n- Email service (SMTP)\n\n### Infrastructure Requirements\n- **Minimum:** 2 CPU cores, 4GB RAM, 50GB storage\n- **Recommended:** 4 CPU cores, 8GB RAM, 100GB storage\n- **Production:** 8+ CPU cores, 16GB+ RAM, 500GB+ storage\n\n---\n\n## Initial Setup\n\n### 1. Clone Repository\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/your-org/prooflink.git\ncd prooflink\n```\n\n### 2. Configure Environment\n```bash\n# Copy production environment template\ncp deployment/production.env .env\n\n# Edit with your values\nnano .env\n```\n\n**Critical values to change:**\n- `DATABASE_URL` - PostgreSQL connection string\n- `REDIS_URL` - Redis connection string\n- `SECRET_KEY` - Random 32+ character string\n- `STRIPE_SECRET_KEY` - Your Stripe secret key\n- `SMTP_*` - Email configuration\n\n### 3. Generate Secrets\n```bash\n# Generate SECRET_KEY\nopenssl rand -hex 32\n\n# Generate database password\nopenssl rand -base64 32\n\n# Generate Redis password\nopenssl rand -base64 32\n```\n\n---\n\n## Docker Deployment\n\n### 1. Build Images\n```bash\n# Build backend\ndocker build -f Dockerfile.backend -t prooflink/backend:latest .\n\n# Build frontend\ndocker build -f Dockerfile.frontend -t prooflink/frontend:latest .\n```\n\n### 2. Start Services\n```bash\n# Start all services\ndocker-compose up -d\n\n# Check status\ndocker-compose ps\n\n# View logs\ndocker-compose logs -f\n```\n\n### 3. Initialize Database\n```bash\n# Run migrations\ndocker-compose exec backend alembic upgrade head\n\n# Create admin user\ndocker-compose exec backend python scripts/create_admin.py\n```\n\n### 4. Verify Deployment\n```bash\n# Check backend health\ncurl http://localhost:8000/health\n\n# Check frontend\ncurl http://localhost:3000\n\n# Check API docs\nopen http://localhost:8000/docs\n```\n\n---\n\n## Kubernetes Deployment\n\n### 1. Create Namespace\n```bash\nkubectl apply -f k8s/namespace.yml\n```\n\n### 2. Configure Secrets\n```bash\n# Edit secrets with your values\nnano k8s/secrets.yml\n\n# Apply secrets\nkubectl apply -f k8s/secrets.yml\n```\n\n### 3. Deploy Database & Cache\n```bash\n# Deploy PostgreSQL\nkubectl apply -f k8s/postgres-statefulset.yml\n\n# Deploy Redis\nkubectl apply -f k8s/redis-deployment.yml\n\n# Wait for ready\nkubectl wait --for=condition=ready pod -l app=postgres -n prooflink --timeout=300s\nkubectl wait --for=condition=ready pod -l app=redis -n prooflink --timeout=300s\n```\n\n### 4. Deploy Application\n```bash\n# Deploy backend\nkubectl apply -f k8s/backend-deployment.yml\n\n# Deploy frontend\nkubectl apply -f k8s/frontend-deployment.yml\n\n# Wait for ready\nkubectl wait --for=condition=ready pod -l app=backend -n prooflink --timeout=300s\nkubectl wait --for=condition=ready pod -l app=frontend -n prooflink --timeout=300s\n```\n\n### 5. Configure Ingress\n```bash\n# Install cert-manager (if not already installed)\nkubectl apply -f https://github.com/cert-manager/cert-manager/releases/download/v1.13.0/cert-manager.yaml\n\n# Apply ingress\nkubectl apply -f k8s/ingress.yml\n```\n\n### 6. Run Database Migrations\n```bash\nkubectl exec -it deployment/backend -n prooflink -- alembic upgrade head\n```\n\n### 7. Verify Deployment\n```bash\n# Check all pods\nkubectl get pods -n prooflink\n\n# Check services\nkubectl get svc -n prooflink\n\n# Check ingress\nkubectl get ingress -n prooflink\n\n# View logs\nkubectl logs -f deployment/backend -n prooflink\n```\n\n---\n\n## Monitoring Setup\n\n### 1. Deploy Prometheus\n```bash\n# Create monitoring namespace\nkubectl create namespace monitoring\n\n# Deploy Prometheus\nkubectl apply -f deployment/monitoring/prometheus.yml -n monitoring\n```\n\n### 2. Deploy Grafana\n```bash\n# Deploy Grafana\nkubectl apply -f deployment/monitoring/grafana.yml -n monitoring\n\n# Get admin password\nkubectl get secret grafana -n monitoring -o jsonpath="{.data.admin-password}" | base64 --decode\n```\n\n### 3. Import Dashboards\n```bash\n# Access Grafana\nkubectl port-forward svc/grafana 3000:3000 -n monitoring\n\n# Open http://localhost:3000\n# Import dashboard from deployment/monitoring/grafana-dashboard.json\n```\n\n### 4. Configure Alerts\n```bash\n# Alerts are configured in deployment/monitoring/alerts.yml\n# They will be automatically loaded by Prometheus\n```\n\n---\n\n## Backup & Recovery\n\n### 1. Automated Backups\n```bash\n# Make backup script executable\nchmod +x deployment/backup.sh\n\n# Run backup manually\n./deployment/backup.sh\n\n# Schedule with cron (daily at 2 AM)\necho "0 2 * * * /path/to/deployment/backup.sh" | crontab -\n```\n\n### 2. Manual Backup\n```bash\n# Database\ndocker exec prooflink-postgres pg_dump -U prooflink prooflink > backup.sql\n\n# Uploads\ndocker run --rm -v prooflink_upload_data:/data -v $(pwd):/backup alpine tar czf /backup/uploads.tar.gz -C /data .\n\n# Redis\ndocker exec prooflink-redis redis-cli SAVE\ndocker cp prooflink-redis:/data/dump.rdb ./redis-backup.rdb\n```\n\n### 3. Restore from Backup\n```bash\n# Make restore script executable\nchmod +x deployment/restore.sh\n\n# List available backups\n./deployment/restore.sh\n\n# Restore specific backup\n./deployment/restore.sh 20240115_120000\n```\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n#### 1. Backend Not Starting\n```bash\n# Check logs\ndocker-compose logs backend\n\n# Common causes:\n# - Database connection failed\n# - Redis connection failed\n# - Missing environment variables\n\n# Verify connections\ndocker-compose exec backend python -c "from app.db.database import engine; print(engine)"\n```\n\n#### 2. Database Connection Issues\n```bash\n# Check PostgreSQL status\ndocker-compose exec postgres pg_isready\n\n# Check connection from backend\ndocker-compose exec backend psql $DATABASE_URL -c "SELECT 1"\n\n# Reset database (WARNING: destroys data)\ndocker-compose down -v\ndocker-compose up -d\n```\n\n#### 3. High Memory Usage\n```bash\n# Check container stats\ndocker stats\n\n# Restart services\ndocker-compose restart\n\n# Scale down (K8s)\nkubectl scale deployment backend --replicas=2 -n prooflink\n```\n\n#### 4. Choose from:\n   - **Proof This Page** - Create proof of entire webpage\n   - **Proof Selection** - Create proof of selected text\n   - **Verify Proof** - Verify a proof from clipboard\n\n#### Method 2: Context Menu\n1. Right-click anywhere on a webpage\n2. Select "Create Proof of This Page"\n3. Or right-click on:\n   - Selected text ‚Üí "Create Proof of Selection"\n   - Images ‚Üí "Create Proof of This Image"\n   - Links ‚Üí "Create Proof of This Link"\n\n#### Method 3: Keyboard Shortcuts\n- **Ctrl+Shift+P** (Cmd+Shift+P on Mac) - Create proof of current page\n- **Ctrl+Shift+V** (Cmd+Shift+V on Mac) - Verify proof from clipboard\n\n### Verifying Proofs\n\n1. Copy a proof link to your clipboard\n2. Click the extension icon\n3. Click "Verify Proof"\n4. Click "Save Settings"\n\n### Local Development\nFor local development, use:\n```\nhttp://localhost:8000/api/v1\n```\n\n## Authentication\n\n### Sign In\n1. Click the extension icon\n2. Click "Sign In"\n3. You\'ll be redirected to the ProofLink.AI login page\n4. After signing in, return to the extension\n\n### Sign Out\n1. Click the extension icon\n2. Click the settings icon\n3. Click "Sign Out"\n\n## Privacy\n\nThe extension:\n\n- ‚úì Only sends data when you create or verify proofs\n- ‚úì Does not track your browsing history\n- ‚úì Does not collect personal information\n- ‚úì Uses secure HTTPS connections\n- ‚úì Stores authentication tokens locally\n\nOptional analytics:\n- ‚úó Can be disabled in settings\n- ‚úó Only sends anonymous usage statistics\n- ‚úó No personal data is collected\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Extension Not Working\n\n1.
